style=\"font-size: 14px;color: rgb(136, 136, 136);\">为了备战大雨，北京市已经武装到了井盖。南方周末记者看到夕照寺街附近的井盖上都拴上了麻绳。</span></p></li></ul><section style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><strong><span style=\"font-size: 14px;\">文 | 南方周末记者 罗欢欢</span></strong></section><section style=\"text-align: right;margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><strong><span style=\"font-size: 14px;\">责任编辑 | 张玥</span></strong></section><section style=\"text-align: right;margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><strong><span style=\"font-size: 14px;\"><br></span></strong></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\">2020年8月12日，为了备战今年最强大雨，整个北京都铆足了劲。</span></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><br></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\">近15万人参与备勤，关闭景区191家、封闭山区道路206条，公交停运192条，工程停工2829个，取消航班400余架次，5574家民宿暂停营业，北京防汛办更是史无前例地倡议“居家办公”。</span></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><br></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\">“这场雨到底有多大？”成了这一天最大的悬念。九点晚高峰已经过去，大雨才姗姗来迟。此刻，留给它的只有一座空城，连国贸、三里屯原本寸步难行的地区，都变得一路畅通。</span></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><br></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\">午夜时分，北京市气象台揭晓了最终答案，12日11时至23时30分降水量（</span><span style=\"font-size: 14px;color: rgb(178, 178, 178);\">毫米</span><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\">）：全市平均55.0，城区平均85.3，西南63.1，西北53.3，东南40.2，东北32.6，城区及全市最大雨量均为海淀香山151.6。</span></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><br></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\">按照雨量分级标准，当24小时累计雨量超过50毫米为暴雨，超过100毫米为大暴雨，超过250毫米为特大暴雨。按照这一标准，此轮大雨达到了暴雨级别，局部地区达到了大暴雨。</span></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><br></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\">不过，这种降雨强度对北京并不罕见，历史上最强降雨出现在2016年7月20日。当时全市平均降雨210.7毫米，城区274.0毫米，其中最大降雨出现在门头沟东山村453.2毫米。</span></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><br></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><img data-ratio=\"1.048\" data-type=\"png\" data-w=\"1000\" 600px\"></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"font-size: 12px;color: rgb(178, 178, 178);\">气象台降水图显示，本轮降水的重地在邢台和保定。</span><br></section><section border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><section style=\"padding-right: 2px;padding-bottom: 2px;padding-left: 2px;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;font-family: inherit;letter-spacing: 0.544px;text-decoration: inherit;display: inline-block;border-color: rgb(95, 1, 1);border-bottom-width: 2px;border-bottom-style: solid;line-height: 1;text-align: center;color: rgb(255, 255, 255);word-wrap: break-word !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><section style=\"padding: 0.3em 0.4em;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;display: inline-block;min-width: 1.8em;min-height: 1.6em;border-radius: 80% 100% 90% 20%;line-height: 1;font-family: inherit;background-color: rgb(95, 1, 1);word-wrap: break-word !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><section style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;font-size: 16px;word-wrap: break-word !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;font-size: 16px;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">1</span></section></section><span style=\"margin-left: 0.4em;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;display: inline-block;line-height: 1.4;font-weight: bolder;text-decoration: inherit;color: rgb(95, 1, 1);font-size: 16px;word-wrap: break-word !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><h3 style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;\"> <span style=\"margin-left: 0.4em;display: inline-block;line-height: 1.4;font-weight: bolder;text-decoration: inherit;color: rgb(95, 1, 1);max-width: 100%;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\">等雨来</span></span></strong></h3></span></section></section></section></section></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\"><br></span></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\">朋友圈是北京市民们集体等雨的地方。8月12日清晨五点半，盲人周彤把手伸出窗外，连毛毛雨都没有摸到。她怒发了一个朋友圈，“雨呢？鸽了吗？我宣布再等你三小时”。</span></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><br></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\">三个小时后，阳光依然灿烂。募旗国泰（</span><span style=\"font-size: 14px;color: rgb(178, 178, 178);\">北京</span><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\">）投资基金管理有限公司积极响应了防汛办的倡议，放了一天“暴雨假”。早上八点半，公司一位员工眼看着雨滴都没见，在微博感叹“休息得好不踏实”。</span></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><br></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\">北京白领女孩邵思思的单位也通知早上可以不用来，可是一早上过去了，雨还没有来，“雨呢？雨呢？雨呢？说好的雨呢？”</span></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><br></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\">直到中午前后，北京才下起分散性雷阵雨。家住顺义的滴滴司机高师傅8月11日提早一个小时收车躲雨，8月12日中午十二点一觉醒来没想到“地还是干的”。把车开到望京，他才短暂经历了一阵小雨。附近六十多个滴滴叫车单，算上他就只有四台优享快车。高师傅听说好多司机担心暴雨没出车。</span></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><br></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\">对高师傅这样的老司机而言，下凹桥的警示线就是一条生命线，积水超过27厘米就不能通行。2012年“721北京特大暴雨”后，为避免再发生积水导致车辆在低洼地被淹事故，交管部门开始对全市易积水的下凹式立交桥、公路、铁路立交桥等施划积水水位警示、警戒标线。</span></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><br></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\">这是一条用生命换来的警示线。2012年北京市民丁志健就在二环内的广渠门下凹桥下逝去。此后，北京主城区再未发生过类似事件。</span></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><br></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\">本轮大雨备战中，广渠门桥布下重兵把守。</span></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><br></section><section style=\"text-align: center;margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><img class=\"rich_pages\" data-ratio=\"0.65234375\" data-s=\"300,640\" data-type=\"jpeg\" data-w=\"1280\" style=\"max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/Tjnia6K0WAwxRhzD5C9mveqrzW8icgsY7OyFOOKUmKljbDLIVg45ctkicy0zsGscwfuHYSLZxibfCh2jy3SFHZiboIA/640?wx_fmt=jpeg\"></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"font-size: 12px;color: rgb(178, 178, 178);\">丁志健八年前溺亡的广渠门桥，每到下雨天都会成为重兵把守之地。</span></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><br></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\">当年出事的桥洞旁边的辅路上，停了三辆警车和一辆清障车，至少布置了十名警察。此外，现场还有一名交警和两名身着北京排水集团马甲的工人。路边堆放着崭新的救生圈、救生衣、救生绳索，以及雨靴等救援设施。</span></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><br></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\">广渠门四个方向的桥洞下，每个方向都安排了两名辅警，他们是15万备战大军中的一员。一名辅警告诉南方周末记者，他主要职责就是看看路面上是否有积水，等了一天雨还没下下来，什么时候下班还得再等领导通知。</span></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><br></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\">各大桥底和重要路口都可以看到正在执勤的警察。据北京青年报消息，为迎战本轮降水，二、三、四环路桥下路口、易积水点段，近三年92处易积水点段和158座下凹桥等点位，全部安排了民警现场备勤。</span></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><br></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\">环卫工人们也处于备勤状态。龙潭环卫所的曲师傅在价值十几万的洗地车内等雨。这种车只在雨天出动，前面喷水后面吸水。曲师傅来来回回磨了一天，地面磨得锃亮反光。他所在的工作群下发最新通知说，大雨将在夜间突袭，今晚谁也不能离开宿舍，一旦出现积水随时都要出动。</span></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><br></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\">为了备战大雨，北京市已经武装到了井盖。南方周末记者看到夕照寺街附近的井盖上都拴上了麻绳。一位附近的居民告诉南方周末记者，早上上班之后，东城交通大队的工作人员就拿着麻绳勾在井盖上，据说下雨后水会顺着麻绳流入井盖内，防止积水。他在这边住了很多年，也是第一次看到这种操作。</span></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><br></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\">中午12点左右，才出现“成建制”的大雨，但来也匆匆去也匆匆。从12时至13时，全市平均降雨量1.3毫米，城区平均降雨量2.5毫米。</span></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><br></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\">晚上19点左右，北京市气象台副台长于波在微博直播时向网友解释，中午出现的第一波降雨，是在偏南暖湿气流下出现的“暖区降雨”，因此降雨分布得很不均匀。</span></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><br></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\">于波说，第二波降雨主要降雨时段是19时之后，最明显的降雨应该出现在22时至凌晨2时，“这一波降雨实际上是由于东移高空槽带来的冷空气与副热带高压外围的切变线带来的暖湿水汽相结合而产生的明显降雨。之所以会比预计的晚一些，实际上就是因为冷空气走得慢了一些，大部队现在还停留在雄安！”</span></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><br></section><section style=\"text-align: center;margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><img class=\"rich_pages\" data-ratio=\"0.68359375\" data-s=\"300,640\" data-type=\"jpeg\" data-w=\"1280\" style=\"max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz_jpg/Tjnia6K0WAwxRhzD5C9mveqrzW8icgsY7OBB7M3tmM4CKRI8ibohfjIYul9O3W11xXXM9xoT0SrBHJUEibb9XI0icuw/640?wx_fmt=jpeg\"></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"font-size: 12px;color: rgb(178, 178, 178);\">晚上六点，等待了一天的救援车辆仍在严阵以待</span><br></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><br></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;font-family: -apple-system-font, BlinkMacSystemFont, \" helvetica neue sc sans gb yahei ui arial sans-serif normal rgb border-box break-word><section style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><section style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><section style=\"max-width: 100%;margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><section style=\"padding-right: 2px;padding-bottom: 2px;padding-left: 2px;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;font-family: inherit;letter-spacing: 0.544px;text-decoration: inherit;display: inline-block;border-color: rgb(95, 1, 1);border-bottom-width: 2px;border-bottom-style: solid;line-height: 1;text-align: center;color: rgb(255, 255, 255);word-wrap: break-word !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><section style=\"padding: 0.3em 0.4em;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;display: inline-block;min-width: 1.8em;min-height: 1.6em;border-radius: 80% 100% 90% 20%;line-height: 1;font-family: inherit;background-color: rgb(95, 1, 1);word-wrap: break-word !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><section style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;font-size: 16px;word-wrap: break-word !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">2</span></section></section><span style=\"margin-left: 0.4em;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;display: inline-block;line-height: 1.4;font-weight: bolder;text-decoration: inherit;color: rgb(95, 1, 1);font-size: 16px;word-wrap: break-word !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><h3 style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;\">  <span style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\">“这雨下得多有素质”</span></span></strong></h3></span></section></section></section></section></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><br></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\">整个白天天空一度放晴，直到入夜后大雨才姗姗来迟。降雨依然造成了一定程度的交通中断。</span></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><br></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\">北京排水集团的数据显示，截至23时15分，排水集团防汛保障范围内丰台区京周路十中门前（</span><span style=\"font-size: 14px;color: rgb(178, 178, 178);\">长辛店北口</span><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\">）、张仪村北口、云岗西路、大灰厂路，海淀区南沙窝桥、安宁庄西路、上清桥东南侧、西客站东西隧道，昌平区育知东路，朝阳区金泰桥等10处由于雨强较大，道路积水30厘米以上，道路交通暂时中断。</span></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><br></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\">早在7月31日，北京也曾出现了一轮降水，主要集中在朝阳北部。25个监测站一度达到暴雨级别，四元桥站一小时雨量已达107毫米。这场局部暴雨造成了7处积水断路，其中四元桥积水2米，交通一度中断了5个小时，直到夜里9点才通车。这一轮降水断路的时间正好在晚高峰之前，导致朝阳北部交通出现严重堵塞。</span></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><br></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\">8月9日，北京也下了一场雨，上清桥西南角积水断路经过2个小时抢险才通车，此外中心城区还有10处积水。</span></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><br></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\">尽管这两场雨无论是规模还是强度，都远不如8月12日的最强降雨，给交通产生了实际影响，也为此轮降水前的“郑重其事”埋下伏笔。</span></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><br></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\">北京统计年鉴显示，北京排水管网总长度从1980年的1423km增长到2015年的 15528km，其中雨水管道从1989年的766km增加到2015年的6139km。</span></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><br></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\">尽管排水长度一直在增加，但是整体上排水管网设计标准偏低。</span></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><br></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\">管网排水标准以“几年一遇”为标准，意思是根据当地的水文资料，推算出几年一遇的最大降雨量。</span></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><br></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\">目前，北京城区管网排水标准一般为排水干线1年一遇左右，城市环路1～2年一遇，中心城区88座雨水泵站重现期小于等于2年的有65座，占73．8% 。</span></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><br></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\">2004年，北京雨水管道规划设计标准为1-3年，重要及特别重要地区为3-5年。参照来看，纽约雨水管道规划设计标准采用10年，伦敦和巴黎采用5年，上海主城区和新城采用的是5年。</span></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><br></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\">2017年北京市实施了新的《城镇雨水系统规划设计暴雨径流计算标准》，北京市雨水管道规划设计标准提高到3-5年，重要及特别重要地区为5-10年。</span></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><br></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\">这轮最强降雨并未给首都“添堵”，强降雨时段在8月12日19时至次日2时，2时之后降雨逐渐减弱，8时前后结束。“既不影响今天的晚高峰，也不影响明天的早高峰，”一位中国气象局的工作人员对此调侃，“这雨下得多有素质。”</span></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><br></section><section style=\"margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;\"><span style=\"font-size: 16px;\">这场事先张扬的大雨将北京气象台置于舆论的漩涡之中。午夜降雨结果出来之后，北京气象台微博转发了一条网友评论：“小编终于扬眉吐气”。</span><img data-ratio=\"0.95\" data-w=\"20\" data-type=\"jpeg\" width=\"auto\" style=\"font-size: 16px; letter-spacing: 0.544px; text-align: right; font-weight: 700; box-sizing: border-box !important; word-wrap: break-word !important; overflow-wrap: break-word !important; visibility: visible !important; width: 20px !important; max-width: 600px\" src=\"http://img2.jintiankansha.me/get?src=http://mmbiz.qpic.cn/mmbiz/Tjnia6K0WAwzba8EO9B3iaHfeyH26BSjDNpv1BPC0M5Uv93otmvZB7VF7kXIZC06STC6BkC7FYqJwaCic7k2fJQHg/640?wx_fmt=jpeg\"></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;letter-spacing: 0.544px;min-height: 1em;text-align: center;margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(114, 114, 114);font-size: 16px;font-weight: 700;letter-spacing: 2px;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;\">其他人都在看：</span></section><section style=\"max-width: 100%;letter-spacing: 0.544px;font-size: 16px;margin-left: 8px;margin-right: 8px;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><section style=\"margin-top: 10px;max-width: 100%;letter-spacing: 0.544px;display: flex;justify-content: center;align-items: center;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><section data-width=\"100%\" style=\"margin-top: -20px;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;width: 329.609px;border-bottom: 1px solid rgb(114, 114, 114);word-wrap: break-word !important;\"></section><section style=\"margin-right: auto;margin-left: auto;padding-right: 5px;padding-left: 5px;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;word-wrap: break-word !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><section style=\"margin-top: -2px;margin-right: auto;margin-left: auto;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;height: 0px;width: 0px;border-style: !important;\">Q：购买后是否有时限？能否下载？</span></p><p style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;font-variant-numeric: normal;letter-spacing: 0.544px;line-height: 27px;word-wrap: break-word !important;\">Q：购买后在哪里听课？找不着课或者课程链接失效了，怎么办？</span></p><p style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-variant-numeric: normal;letter-spacing: 0.544px;line-height: 27.2px;box-sizing: border-box !important;\">A：能。在电脑的微信端可以直接打开，或者复制课程链接，用微信扫描登录后可看。如果手机与电视都支持“投屏”功能的话，也可在电视上观看。</p><p style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;font-variant-numeric: normal;letter-spacing: !important;\">请点击课程页面上的“送好友”功能后再支付。</p><p style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;font-variant-numeric: normal;letter-spacing: 0.544px;line-height: 27px;word-wrap: break-word style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;\">聚美</strong>，你可能会很自然地想起“我为自己代言”，但未必知道<strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;\">他们的“英雄谱”里曾藏着一位大神，4个月创造从0到1.52亿的商业奇迹</strong>。</span></p><p style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;word-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;word-wrap: break-word powered-by=\"xiumi.us\" style=\"padding-right: 5px;padding-left: 5px;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;line-height: 2;font-size: 15px;word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><p style=\"max-width: !important;\">他是前京东集团副总裁、前聚美POP事业部总经理......</strong></span></p><p style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"max-width: break-word !important;\">从电话销售做起</span>，先后做到了企划经理、企划总监，短短一年就有了自己的独立办公室和秘书。</span></p></section><section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\" style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><p style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;word-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;word-wrap: break-word powered-by=\"xiumi.us\" style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><p style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;word-wrap: break-word 5px;max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;font-size: 15px;line-height: 2;word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><p style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;word-wrap: break-word !important;\">如果说从小白到总监，老路这一路“势如破竹”，那加入聚美的他，就更是“有如神助”。</p><p style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: 70, 75);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;\">2012年10月底，老路加入聚美，据悉，他所分管的业务，之前的销售额一天<span style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;word-wrap: break-word !important;\">顶多</span>也就3万，对比整个公司的销售额，几乎可以忽略不计。</span></p><p style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;word-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(65, 70, 75);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;\">他花了4个月的时间，从零开始，对这块业务进行了<span style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;word-wrap: break-word !important;\">各方位</span>改造。决策方向把控上，他运筹帷幄；指挥团队作战上，他有条不紊，短短几个月的时间，展现了<span style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;word-wrap: break-word !important;\">非凡</span>的领导力、创造力。</span></p><p style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;word-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(65, 70, 75);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;\">2013年3月1日当天，该业务板块<strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;\">仅单天的销售额就高达1.52亿人民币</strong>，已与4个月前的3万不可同日而语了。</span></p><p style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;word-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(65, 70, 75);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;word-wrap: break-word !important;\">鸡汤界有这样一句话：</span><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;word-wrap: break-word !important;\">你<span style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;word-wrap: break-word !important;\">要</span>拼尽全力，才能看上去毫不费力。</strong></span></p><p style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;word-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(65, 70, 75);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;word-wrap: break-word !important;\">4个月的时间，从0到1.52亿。</strong></span></p><p style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: 70, 75);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;\">从整个部门的招聘、培训，到商家招募、商品组织、规则制定、页面优化，老路每一步的艰辛，旁人可能无法感同身受，但他付出的心血之多，每个跟他并肩战斗过的伙伴，都不言自明。</span></p><p style=\"max-width: !important;\">但他没有被盛誉冲昏头脑，也没有沉溺于过往辉煌。面对公司给出的一纸期权，他毅然放弃，选择回归校园，读书深造。</p></section><section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\" style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><p !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;color: rgb(224, 59, 59);word-wrap: break-word !important;\">回归校园攻读清华MBA</span></strong></p></section><section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\" style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><p style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(65, 70, 75);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;\">后来，聚美在纽交所上市，<span style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;word-wrap: break-word !important;\">在股价峰顶高点时</span>，这一纸期权，价值超过了一个亿。</span></p><p style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(65, 70, 75);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;word-wrap: break-word !important;\">当一个亿假以时日真的摆在自己面前</span>，的确很难割舍。更难割舍的，是自己“读书的梦想”。</span></p><p style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(65, 70, 75);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;\">就连同事们都不知道，在创造1.52亿这个奇迹的同时，老路还在做着另一件大事——<strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;\">备考清华大学MBA的全国笔试</strong>。</span></p><p style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;word-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(65, 70, 75);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;\">因为好多年没有碰书本了，笔试对老路而言，压力并不小。</span></p><p style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;word-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: !important;\">每天中午背1个小时单词，下班后在一个咖啡厅的固定位置，看书备考到凌晨1点，<span style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;word-wrap: break-word !important;\">次日</span>再去公司带着团队冲刺，每天如此往复，直到考前一天。</span></p><p border-box;word-wrap: break-word !important;\">他</span>得了中度抑郁，后来靠<span style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;word-wrap: break-word !important;\">医药</span>的辅助，才一点点恢复过来。</span></p><p break-word !important;\">每天6小时泡图书馆，研究商业案例，大年三十，吃口饺子就赶紧背单词，恶补英语、恶补<span style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;word-wrap: break-word !important;\">学业</span>知识。</span></p><p style=\"max-width: !important;\">这是他功成名就以后，还能干出来的事情。</span></p><p style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: !important;\">这一关他挺过来了。</strong></span></p><p style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(65, 70, 75);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;\">2017年，音频课程《用得上的商学课》上线。</span></p><p style=\"max-width: border-box;color: rgb(65, 70, 75);word-wrap: break-word !important;\">2019年，音频课累计付费用户超过80万，销售额突破8000万。同年，中信出版同名书发售。</span></p><p style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(65, 70, 75);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;\">2019年7月，品牌升级为【小商业】。</span></p><p break-word !important;\">2019年10月，《初级商业特训营》上线。</span></p><p style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;color: rgb(65, 70, 75);word-wrap: break-word !important;\">你可能会疑惑，<strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;\">商业和普通人有什么关系，为什么人人都要学点商业知识</strong>？</span></p><p style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;word-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: !important;\">老路这样解释：我们这一代人，所有的焦虑</span>，<span style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;word-wrap: break-word !important;\">都来自于我们把珍贵的一切</span>，投资给了别人，投资给了外物，而舍不得，投资一点点，给我们自己。</span></p><p style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;word-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p break-word !important;\">你投资房子，投资车子。<span style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;word-wrap: break-word !important;\">你投资圈子，投资孩子。</span></span></p><p style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(65, 70, 75);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;word-wrap: break-word !important;\">你，有多久没有投资你自己了？</strong></span></p></section><section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\" style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: 70, 75);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;\">名校MBA毕业生的平均年薪是45万。清华北大MBA毕业，年薪破百万的，车载斗量，不可胜数。<span style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;word-wrap: break-word !important;\">而读完MBA，需要超群的能力、胆识、品德。</span></span></p><p style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: !important;\">为什么这么有价值的内容，不是每个人都能学到呢</strong>？</span></p><p style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: 70, 75);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;word-wrap: break-word !important;\">首先</span>，名校MBA都有<strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;\">工作年限的要求</strong>，一般要求5年以上工作经验，3年以上管理经验，这就让一大批刚刚步入职场的年轻人，无法企及。</span></p><p style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;word-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(65, 70, 75);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;word-wrap: break-word !important;\">其次</span>，名校MBA不但学费不菲，动辄二三十万起，<span style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;word-wrap: break-word !important;\">更重要的是</span>，全日制的学习，需要你<strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;\">两到三年完全放弃工作和收入</strong>，全身心回到校园，这就让一大批有家庭负担的人群，望而却步。</span></p><p style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;word-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(65, 70, 75);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;\">老路希望，这些商业知识，不再是商界大佬和成功人士的私人订制课程，也不再是动辄几十万的天价学费，将人拒之门外。</span></p><p style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;word-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;color: rgb(65, 70, 75);word-wrap: break-word !important;\">如果你不希望职业生涯受制于现有的认知视野和思维格局，不妨和老路一起学习这门《<strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;\">老路：用得上的商学课</strong>》。</span></p><p style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;word-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(65, 70, 75);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><strong style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;word-wrap: break-word !important;\">在这里，生意场上真实鲜活的案例，商家不为人知的诀窍，和那些埋头攒钱的人，永远不会知道的赚钱秘密，老路告诉你。</strong></span></p><p style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;color: rgb(65, 70, 75);box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;\">老路的商学课<span style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;word-wrap: break-word !important;\">讲的</span>不只是具体知识，更是一种思维<span style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;word-wrap: break-word !important;\">的</span>方式，是身处商业社会里，<span style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;word-wrap: break-word !important;\">大多数人</span>尚未达到的格局观。</span></p><p style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p></section><section powered-by=\"xiumi.us\" style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;word-wrap: break-word !important;\"><section border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;\">请问怎么试听试看呀？</span><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box !important;word-wrap: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"max-width: !important;\">A：点击二维码进入“南周书院”店铺后，选择相关产品点开，在“目录”中选择标有“试听/试看”的内容即可。</p><p style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;font-variant-numeric: normal;letter-spacing: 0.544px;line-height: !important;\"></p><p style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;font-variant-numeric: normal;letter-spacing: 0.544px;line-height: 27px;word-wrap: break-word !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;color: rgb(255, 129, 36);word-wrap: break-word !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">Q：购买后是否有时限？能否下载？</span></p><p style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;font-variant-numeric: normal;letter-spacing: 0.544px;line-height: 27px;word-wrap: break-word !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">A：一旦购买可以反复回听/回看。但是不能下载。</p><p style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;font-variant-numeric: normal;letter-spacing: break-word !important;\"></p><p style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;font-variant-numeric: normal;letter-spacing: 0.544px;line-height: 27px;word-wrap: break-word !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><span style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;color: rgb(255, 129, 36);word-wrap: break-word !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">Q：购买后在哪里听课？找不着课或者课程链接失效了，怎么办？</span></p><p style=\"max-width: 100%;min-height: 1em;font-variant-numeric: normal;letter-spacing: 0.544px;line-height: 27.2px;box-sizing: border-box break-word !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">A：请进入\"南方周末\"公众号，点击菜单栏\"南周严选\"-\"南周书院\"-\"我的\"-\"我的已购\"，可找到您所购买的课程。</span></p><p style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: 1em;font-variant-numeric: normal;letter-spacing: 0.544px;line-height: 27px;word-wrap: break-word !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\">A：能。在电脑的微信端可以直接打开，或者复制课程链接，用微信扫描登录后可看。如果手机与电视都支持“投屏”功能的话，也可在电视上观看。</p><p style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;font-variant-numeric: normal;letter-spacing: 0.544px;line-height: 27px;word-wrap: break-word !important;overflow-wrap: break-word !important;\"><br style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;word-wrap: break-word !important;overflow-wrap: !important;\">请点击课程页面上的“送好友”功能后再支付。</p><p style=\"max-width: 100%;box-sizing: border-box;min-height: 1em;font-variant-numeric: normal;letter-spacing: 0.544px;line-height: 27px;word-wrap: break-word
